<h1 style='margin-left:0cm;text-indent:0cm;page-break-before:always'><a
name="__RefHeading___Toc4167_1962934934"></a><a name="_xzfrmvz5emeq"></a><span
lang=EN-US>Purpose </span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>This
document provides specifics that describes the application that is to be used
to orchestrate the processing of employee based events.Â  This application will
receive a MQSeries message and use the payload of the message to identify, and
then orchestrate any API calls required to facilitate the processing, and
eventual consumption of the employee event.</span></p>

<h1 style='margin-left:0cm;text-indent:0cm'><a
name="__RefHeading___Toc4169_1962934934"></a><a name="_91up5ftfq38u"></a><a
name="_duaiaqmiux43"></a><span lang=EN-US>Taxonomy</span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>zDirectory</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>: An application used to
support claim hold triggered by litigation. </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>HCM</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>: Human Capital Management
system which is PeopleSoft</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Active
Directory</span></b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>:
System of record for employee account information</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Buyers
Quest</span></b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>:
Enterprise corporate procurement application</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>B2BI</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>: McLaneÂs application for
handling bulk data</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Egencia</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>: McLaneÂs travel agency
application</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Shiftboard</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>: Cloud application to
support distribution center shift management</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h1 style='margin-left:0cm;text-indent:0cm;page-break-before:always'><a
name="__RefHeading___Toc4179_1962934934"></a><a name="_1fjph8wid7xq"></a><span

<h2><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4181_1962934934"></a><a name="_srao1hb0zonx"></a><span
lang=EN-US>Employee Event Synchronization</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-right:-9.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-right:-9.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Employee events synchronization
orchestration strives to make employee events consumable by interested
applications.Â  This typically required data enrichment, process step
orchestration,Â Â  format ,mediation, and delivery over various protocols.Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-right:-9.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Initially, this application is to be
built to support the following:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-9.0pt;margin-bottom:
0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span

<h2><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4183_1962934934"></a><a name="_5vi1wtep679l"></a><span
lang=EN-US>Functional Design</span></h2>

<h3><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4185_1962934934"></a><a name="_2iouclshyu8u"></a><a
name="_7gxwd1j5k2od"></a><span lang=EN-US>Resources</span></h3>

<h4><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4187_1962934934"></a><a name="_mstgbo4hwb5"></a><a
name="_kds4ax6do0n4"></a><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Employee
Event Synchronization</span></h4>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>This
application will be responsible for the orchestration of the required
processing, and mediation steps to insure that employee event information is
prepared, and presented to downstream applications for their consumption.Â  This
processing will be triggered by details obtained from the payload of a message
from a MQSeries queue.Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h5><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4189_1962934934"></a><span lang=EN-US>Project
Names:</span></h5>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>OAS
Model Project: Does Not Apply</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Development
Project: employee-events-sync-prc-app</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>OpenShift
Project: employee-events-dev, employee-events-test, employee-events</span></p>

lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;

<h5><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4197_1962934934"></a><a name="_4vs02rdnrkwj"></a><span
lang=EN-US>Processing </span></h5>

<h6><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4199_1962934934"></a><span lang=EN-US>Processing
Structure:</span></h6>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Right after the On New Message source
component, wrap any ÂlooseÂ components on the palette in a try block and place
any related special error processing in the ÂError handlingÂ/ÂCatchÂ section.Â 
In our case, we would like to log the error, but in the future, we may want to
store the original message in a queue for later use.Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The main reason for doing this is to
prevent a poison message situation where upon failure, the message rolls back
to the input queue, and then picked up again for processing placing us in a
loop.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>The main ÂError handlingÂ/ÂCatchÂ section
should contain an On Error Continue component to catch ANY type of error and
should simply just log the error details as well as the payload.Â  The key thing
about this</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>In General the flow template should look
like so:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><img border=0 width=625 height=259
src="TSD-Employee%20Events%20Orchestration%20Handler%20Process%20APP%20Interactions-v1.8.1.files/image033.jpg"></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h6><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4211_1962934934"></a><span lang=EN-US>Validation</span></h6>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>The
following fields are mandatory and should be checked to insure they are present
on the request payload</span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New"'>o<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>employees
Â at least one item in the collection</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Â Â Â Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New"'>o<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>employees.employeeId
must be present, and not null</span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-left:36.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Courier New"'>o<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>eventAction
</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>must
be present, and not null</span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-left:36.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>If any of
these fields are missing, log the standard status message with the following
fields</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>status.code = Â400Â</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>status.messages.type=ÂErrorÂ</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>status.messages.message =
Required field {field} is missing from the request</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>status.messages.context =
app.name</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-13.5pt;
margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<h6><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4213_1962934934"></a><span lang=EN-US>eventAction
= &quot;AddressbookSync&quot;</span></h6>

<p class=MsoHeading7><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4215_1962934934"></a><span
lang=EN-US>Step 1: Get employee account information from Active Directory</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>If eventAction=AddressbookSync and email</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;color:black'> does not
contain &quot;noreply&quot;</span><span lang=EN-US> then perform this step to
enhance the incoming employee data with the one drive url value from active
directory</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>For each item in the employees collection </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>If
employees[*].employeeId is present, and not null call the Active Directory
system API to get the oneDriveURL for the employee</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Â Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Call the Active Directory System API: <a
href="#_toc3364">#Get employee account information from Active
Directory|outline</a></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Success:
Proceed to the next step</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.25pt;background:#FFFFFE'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>Failure:
Capture error context, write the error to the log, and continue on to Step#2</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;line-height:14.25pt;
background:#FFFFFE'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading7><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4227_1962934934"></a><span
lang=EN-US>Step 1a: Enhance the incoming request from the active directory
response data:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-userId</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-One drive url</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-Single sign on id</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-TravelGroup</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-<span style='color:black;background:yellow'>purchasingApprovalGroup</span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-<span style='color:black;background:yellow'>approvalLimitAmount</span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;line-height:14.25pt;
background:#FFFFFE'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>Example Response from the
Active directory system API</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>Add the above elements returned
from the Active Directory system API response to employee item of the incoming
employees collection.Â  If the response from the Active Directory system API
does not contain a value for any of these elements, assign ÂÂ as a value when
adding it the employee item of the employees collection</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>Special assignment for
Travel group:</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:black'>For teammates with no
McLane email (employee.email contains &quot;noreply&quot;) instead of assigning
ÂÂ, use the crosswalk file to lookup the travel group by division (Use the

lang=EN-US style='color:#5D5F6E'> </span></b></p>

<p class=MsoHeading7 style='page-break-before:always'><a
name="__RefHeading___Toc4229_1962934934"></a><s><span lang=EN-US>Step 2: Upsert
employee data in bulk into the zDiscovery address book</span></s></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>If eventAction=AddressbookSync then perform
this step</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading8><span lang=EN-US>Call the zDiscovery system API to post
the address book data </span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading9><span lang=EN-US>Resource Locators</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Upsert
employees to Zdiscovery address bookÂ  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>PUT</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Consolas'> </span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>{BASE_URI}/v1/address-book/contacts</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Type of
Data Consumed:Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>application/json</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>See
OAS model project for interaction details: </span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>zdiscovery-litigations-sys-api</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading9><span lang=EN-US>Interact with the zDiscovery system API</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Symbol;
color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>API:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-31.5pt;
margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>PUT</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>
https://&lt;server&gt;:&lt;port&gt;/v1/</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>address-book/contacts</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>?</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;
color:#5D5F6E'>identifyingElementName</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>=xxxxxx</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:Consolas'>Example:</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-31.5pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>PUT</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;
color:#5D5F6E'> https://&lt;server&gt;:&lt;port&gt;/zdiscovery-litigations/v1/</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;
color:#5D5F6E'>address-book/contacts</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:#5D5F6E'>?identifyingElementName=employeeId</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Request Connector Configuration</span></i></b><i><span

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span

</span></span><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Response Timeout(ms): 15000 (responseTimeOut)</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-4.5pt;
margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-4.5pt;
margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Success:
Proceed to the next step</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.25pt;background:#FFFFFE'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>Failure<i>: </i>Capture
error context, write the error to the log, and continue on to Step#3</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;line-height:14.25pt;
background:#FFFFFE'><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoHeading7 style='page-break-before:always'><a
name="__RefHeading___Toc4229_19629349341"></a><span lang=EN-US>Step 3: Get
employee data from EBS</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:black;background:yellow'>If
eventAction=AddressbookSync AND employee.costCenter is null, blank, or is not
on the request then perform this step</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E;background:yellow'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading8><span lang=EN-US>Call the EBS Employee system API to get
employee data </span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading9><span lang=EN-US>Resource Locators</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Get
employee data for a given employee IdentifierÂ  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>GET</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Consolas'> </span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>{BASE_URI}/v1/employees/{employeeId}</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Type of
Data Consumed:Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>application/json</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>See
OAS model project for interaction details: ebs</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>-employees-sys-api</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading9><span lang=EN-US>Interact with the EBS Employee system API</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Symbol;
color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>API:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-31.5pt;
margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>GET</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>
https://&lt;server&gt;:&lt;port&gt;/ebs-employees-sys-api/v1/</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>employees/XXXXXXXXX</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:Consolas'>Example:</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-31.5pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>GET</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;
color:#5D5F6E'>
https://&lt;server&gt;:&lt;port&gt;/ebs-employees-sys-api/v1/employees</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;
color:#5D5F6E'>/000135270</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>Example Response:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Request Connector Configuration</span></i></b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>:
(externalize into a property file)</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Response Timeout(ms): 15000 (responseTimeOut)</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-right:-4.5pt'><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:18.0pt;line-height:14.25pt;
background:#FFFFFE'><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Success:
Proceed to the next step</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.25pt;background:#FFFFFE'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>Failure:
Capture error context, write the error to the log, and continue on to Step#4</span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading7><a name="__RefHeading___Toc1211705_69315954"></a><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt;line-height:115%'><br>
</span><span lang=EN-US>Step 3a: Enhance the incoming request from a successful
EBS Employee response data:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>This step is applicable if the call to EBS
employee system API was made sucessfully</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-Cost Center</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:black;background:yellow'>If
the incoming request does not contain the element employees[*].costCenter or
the value for employees[*].costCenter is null or ÂÂ then assign costCenter from
the EBS employees system</span><span lang=EN-US> <span style='color:black;
background:yellow'>api response</span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:black;background:yellow'>-Manager
Id</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:black;background:yellow'>If
the incoming request does not contain the element employees[*].managerId or the
value for employees[*].managerId is null or ÂÂ then assign managerId from the
EBS employees system</span><span lang=EN-US> <span style='color:black;
background:yellow'>api response</span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:black;background:yellow'>-Location
Id</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:black;background:yellow'>If
the incoming request does not contain the element employees[*].locationId or
the value for employees[*]. locationId is null or ÂÂ then assign locationId
from the EBS employees system</span><span lang=EN-US> <span style='color:black;
background:yellow'>api response</span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>NOTE</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>: These values will be populated when Workday goes live as our HCM
system, so if these elements have values in them, we want to preserve, and use
those values.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>Add the above element(s)
returned from the EBS Employee system API response to theÂ  employee item of the
incoming employees collection.Â  If the response from the EBS Employee system
API does not contain a value for any of these elements, assign ÂÂ as a value
when adding it the employee item of the employees collection</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading7 style='page-break-before:always'><a
name="__RefHeading___Toc4229_19629349342"></a><span lang=EN-US>Step 4:
EgenciaTravel: Post groups of employee data to B2BI to be eventually sent to
Egencia</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>I<span style='color:black;background:yellow'>f</span>
eventAction=AddressbookSync then perform this step</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading8><span lang=EN-US>Call the B2BI Files system API to post
the employee data </span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading8><span lang=EN-US>Resource Locators</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Create
employee records intended for Egencia </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>POST</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Consolas'> </span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>{BASE_URI}/v1/files/employees?</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Type of
Data Consumed:Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>application/json</span></p>

OAS model project for interaction details: </span><span lang=EN-US

  <td width=298 valign=top style='width:223.25pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNoSpacing><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
  "Verdana",sans-serif'>string, Ex. Hines</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading8><span lang=EN-US>Interact with the B2BI system API</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Symbol;
color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>API:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-31.5pt;
margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>POST</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>
https://&lt;server&gt;:&lt;port&gt;/b2bi-files-sys-api/v1/files/</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>employees?targetApplication=xxxxxx</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:Consolas'>Example:</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-31.5pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>POST</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>

ExterroLitigation: Post groups of employee data to B2BI to be eventually sent

the employee data </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Create
employee records intended for Exterro </span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading8><span lang=EN-US>Interact with the B2BI system API</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Symbol;
color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>API:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-31.5pt;
margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US

lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>
https://&lt;server&gt;:&lt;port&gt;/b2bi-files-sys-api/v1/files/</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>employees?targetApplication=xxxxxx</span></p>

</span></span><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:18.0pt;line-height:14.25pt;
background:#FFFFFE'><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></i></p>

<h6 style='page-break-before:always'><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4231_1962934934"></a><span
lang=EN-US>eventAction=Termination</span></h6>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading7 style='page-break-before:always'><a
name="__RefHeading___Toc4215_1962934934_Copy_2"></a><span lang=EN-US>Step 1:
Get employee account information from Active Directory</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>If eventAction=Termination and email</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;color:black'> does not
contain &quot;noreply&quot;</span><span lang=EN-US> then perform this step to
enhance the incoming employee data with values from active directory</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>For each item in the employees collection </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:9.0pt'><span lang=EN-US>If
employees[*].employeeId is present, and not null call the Active Directory
system API to get the user account data for the employee</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Â Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Call the Active Directory System API: <a
href="#_toc3364">#Get employee account information from Active
Directory|outline</a></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Success:
Proceed to the next step</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.25pt;background:#FFFFFE'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>Failure:
Capture error context, write the error to the log, and continue on to Step#2</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.25pt;background:#FFFFFE'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading7><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4227_1962934934_Copy_1"></a><span
lang=EN-US>Step 1a: Enhance the incoming request from the active directory
response data:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-userId</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-One drive url</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-Single sign on id</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>-TravelGroup</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;line-height:14.25pt;
background:#FFFFFE'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>Example Response from the
Active directory system API</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>Add the above elements returned
from the Active Directory system API response to employee item of the incoming
employees collection.Â  If the response from the Active Directory system API
does not contain a value for any of these elements, assign ÂÂ as a value when
adding it the employee item of the employees collection</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>Special assignment for
Travel group:</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:black'>For teammates with no
McLane email (employee.email contains &quot;noreply&quot;) instead of assigning
ÂÂ, use the crosswalk file to lookup the travel group by division (Use the
first five positions of the division element value for the lookup)&nbsp;</span><b><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#5D5F6E'> </span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='color:#5D5F6E'>Crosswalk file : </span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:#5D5F6E'>Example of the resulting
enhanced payload. </span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading7><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4233_1962934934"></a><span
lang=EN-US>Step 2: Call the B2BI system API to post the employee data </span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading8><span lang=EN-US>Resource Locators</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraph style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol;color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Create
an employee termination recordÂ  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>POST</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Consolas'> </span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>{BASE_URI}/v1/files/employees?</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Type of
Data Consumed:Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-left:0cm'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>application/json</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>See
OAS model project for interaction details: </span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>b2bi-files-sys-api</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>&nbsp;</span></p>

<p class=MsoHeading8><span lang=EN-US>Interact with the B2BI system API</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Symbol;
color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>API:</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-31.5pt;
margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>POST</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>
https://&lt;server&gt;:&lt;port&gt;/b2bi-files-sys-api/v1/files/</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>employees?targetApplication=xxxxxx</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:Consolas'>Example:</span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-31.5pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>POST</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>
https://&lt;server&gt;:&lt;port&gt;/b2bi-files-sys-api/v1/files/</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>employees?targetApplication=BuyerQuest</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;
font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>Example Request:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt'>{</span></p>

<p class=MsoNoSpacing><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt'>Â

<p class=MsoNormal><s><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'><span style='text-decoration:
 none'>&nbsp;</span></span></s></p>

<p class=MsoHeading8><s><span lang=EN-US>Interact with the HCM Shift Management
Process API system API</span></s></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt'><s><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Symbol;
color:blue'>Â·<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></s><s><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>API:</span></s></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast style='margin-top:0cm;margin-right:-31.5pt;
margin-bottom:0cm;margin-left:18.0pt;margin-bottom:.0001pt'><s><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;
color:blue'>POST</span></s><s><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'> https://&lt;server&gt;:&lt;port&gt;/v1/</span></s><s><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>employees/supervisors</span></s></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><s><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:Consolas'>Example:</span></s></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-right:-31.5pt'><s><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas;color:blue'>POST</span></s><s><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.5pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Consolas'>

<h6><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4235_1962934934"></a><span lang=EN-US>Logging
the API request, and response: </span></h6>

<p class=MsoHeading7><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4237_1962934934"></a><span
lang=EN-US>Logging Payload:</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>We should log data prior to the API call,
and after the api call.Â  The log message prior to the api call should contain
the resource endpoint being called, the request message payload if it applies,
as well as the standard log elements, and the log message after the api call
should contain the response.Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><s><span lang=EN-US><span style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></span></s></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>At the end of the flow, we should log the
results of the api call with the following elements.</span></p>

  "Verdana",sans-serif'>If http response from the API call starts with a 2</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNoSpacing><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
  "Verdana",sans-serif'>then Success</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNoSpacing><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:
  "Verdana",sans-serif'>else assign the error message</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=217 style='width:162.8pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;

  <p class=MsoNoSpacing style='layout-grid-mode:char'><span lang=EN-US

  </td>

<h6><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4239_1962934934"></a><a name="_6s4zv2xizbks"></a><a
name="_nemugy9pdv1b"></a><span lang=EN-US>Error Processing</span></h6>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>If an issue/error is encountered with this application, the
specifics related to the error are to be reported via logging which will be
routed over to splunk.</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><s><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'><span style='text-decoration:none'>&nbsp;</span></span></s></p>

font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>f there are any issues/errors
returned from this MQ call, the context of the error should be placed in the
status section, and a response should be formatted and sent back to the
caller.Â  </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;
color:black'>-Set the following status elements in the response</span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>status = 500 </span></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpLast><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif;color:black'>context.type =
ÂErrorÂ</span></p>

<h2><a name="__RefHeading___Toc4261_1962934934"></a><a name="_IBM_MQ_Connector"></a><span
lang=EN-US>IBM MQ Connector Configuration</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><b><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>IBM MQ Configuration</span></i></b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>:
(externalize into a property file)</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;
line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><b><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Extension</span></i></b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>:
camel-quarkus-amqp - This extension leverages the Quarkus Qpid JMS extension. A
ConnectionFactory bean is automatically created and wired into the AMQP
component for you. The connection factory can be configured via the Quarkus
Qpid JMS configuration options.</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='line-height:normal'><b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Â Â Â Â 
quarkus.qpid-jms.url=amqp://{host}:{port}</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-right:-13.45pt;line-height:
normal'><b><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>quarkus.qpid-jms.wrap=true</span></i></b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'> (setting
can allow the Qpid JMS extension to apply a ConnectionFactory wrapper supplied
by another extension to the injected ConnectionFactory.Â  Setting this value to
true and adding an additional dependency on quarkus-pooled-jms to your
application allows quarkus-pooled-jms to provide pooling for the injected
ConnectionFactory</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;
line-height:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:Symbol'>Â·<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span><b><i><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>Extension</span></i></b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>:
quarkus-pooled-jms</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:54.0pt;line-height:normal'><b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>quarkus.pooled-jms.pooling.enabled=true</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:54.0pt;line-height:normal'><b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>quarkus.pooled-jms.max-connections=1</span></i></b></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:54.0pt;line-height:normal'><b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>quarkus.pooled-jms.max-sessions-per-connection=10</span></i></b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'> (number
of Sessions that the pooled Connection will loan out before either blocking)</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:54.0pt;line-height:normal'><b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>quarkus.pooled-jms.block-if-session-pool-is-full=true</span></i></b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'> (block
until another previously created and loaned out session is closed an thereby
becomes available)</span></i></p>

<p class=MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle style='margin-left:54.0pt;line-height:normal'><b><i><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:10.0pt;font-family:"Verdana",sans-serif'>quarkus.pooled-jms.block-if-session-pool-is-full-timeout=-1</span></i></b><i><span
